# Requirements Document for 'BookstoreOnline' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'BookstoreOnline' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse books, add items to cart, checkout, write reviews, and track order history. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'BookstoreOnline' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'BookstoreOnline' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Bookstore Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured books, bestsellers, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-books** - Type: Div - Display of featured book recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-catalog-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to book catalog page.
  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bestsellers page.

### 2. Book Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Book Catalog
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available books with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search books by title, author, or ISBN.
  - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Fiction, Non-Fiction, Science, History, etc.).
  - **ID: books-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying book cards with cover, title, author, and price.
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each book card has this).

### 3. Book Details Page
- **Page Title**: Book Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific book.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: book-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the book details page.
  - **ID: book-title** - Type: H1 - Display book title.
  - **ID: book-author** - Type: Div - Display book author.
  - **ID: book-price** - Type: Div - Display book price.
  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add book to shopping cart.
  - **ID: book-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Shopping Cart Page
- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart
- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.
  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with title, quantity, price, and subtotal.
  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.
  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.

### 5. Checkout Page
- **Page Title**: Checkout
- **Overview**: A page for users to enter shipping information and complete purchase.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.
  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: shipping-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input shipping address.
  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).
  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.

### 6. Order History Page
- **Page Title**: Order History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous orders with tracking information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the orders page.
  - **ID: orders-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.
  - **ID: view-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view order details (each order has this).
  - **ID: order-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reviews Page
- **Page Title**: Customer Reviews
- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews and allowing users to write new reviews.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.
  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with book title, rating, and review text.
  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.
  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Write Review Page
- **Page Title**: Write a Review
- **Overview**: A page for users to write reviews for purchased books.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.
  - **ID: select-book** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select book to review.
  - **ID: rating-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).
  - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.
  - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.

### 9. Bestsellers Page
- **Page Title**: Bestsellers
- **Overview**: A page displaying top-selling books ranked by sales.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: bestsellers-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bestsellers page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, and sales count.
  - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (This Week, This Month, All Time).
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each bestseller has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Books Data
- **File Name**: `books.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- **File Name**: `categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
  3|Science|Scientific topics and research
  ```

### 3. Cart Data
- **File Name**: `cart.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2|2025-01-15
  2|3|1|2025-01-16
  ```

### 4. Orders Data
- **File Name**: `orders.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
  ```

### 5. Order Items Data
- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2|12.99
  2|1|3|1|14.99
  3|2|2|1|16.99
  ```

### 6. Reviews Data
- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
  ```

### 7. Bestsellers Data
- **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|sales_count|period
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  2|150|This Month
  1|120|This Month
  3|95|This Month
  ```

# BookstoreOnline Flask Application Design Specification

## 1. Flask Routes

### Root Route
- `/` (GET): redirects to `/dashboard`.

### Dashboard
- Route: `/dashboard` (GET)
- Template: `dashboard.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `featured_books`: List[Dict], each dict contains `book_id` (int), `title` (str), `author` (str), `price` (float)
- Purpose: Display featured recommendations with quick navigation.
- Elements:
  - Container with ID: `dashboard-page`
  - Display container with ID: `featured-books`
  - Button with ID: `browse-catalog-button` (Navigates to `/catalog`)

### Catalog
- Route: `/catalog` (GET)
- Template: `catalog.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `books`: List[Dict], each with `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `category`, `price`
  - `categories`: List[Dict], each with `category_id`, `category_name`, `description`
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `catalog-page`
  - Search input text field: `search-input`
  - Category filter dropdown: `category-filter`
  - Book grid container: `book-grid`
  - Each book card has an ID button: `view-details-button-{book_id}`
- Features: Search by title or author; filter by category (e.g., Science)

### Book Details
- Route: `/book/<int:book_id>` (GET)
- Template: `book_details.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `book`: Dict with detailed book information
  - `reviews`: List[Dict] for the book
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `book-details-page`
  - Book title display (H1 inside main heading)
  - Div with ID: `book-price` to show price
  - Button with ID: `add-to-cart-button` to add book to cart
  - Div with ID: `book-reviews` to display customer reviews
- Form for POST to add to cart

### Shopping Cart
- Route: `/cart` (GET, POST)
- Template: `cart.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `cart_items`: List[Dict], each with `item_id`, `book`, `quantity`
  - `total_amount`: Float
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `cart-page`
  - Cart items displayed in table with ID: `cart-table`
  - Quantity input fields: `update-quantity-{item_id}`
  - Remove buttons: `remove-item-button-{item_id}`
  - Div with ID: `total-amount` showing total cost
  - Button to checkout: `checkout-button`
- POST method handles quantity updates, removals

### Checkout
- Route: `/checkout` (GET, POST)
- Template: `checkout.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `cart_items`, `total_amount`
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `checkout-page`
  - Input field with ID: `shipping-address` for shipping info
  - Payment method dropdown `payment-method` (e.g., Credit Card, PayPal)
  - Button to place order: `place-order-button`
- POST method processes order submission

### Order History
- Route: `/orders` (GET)
- Template: `orders.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `orders`: List[Dict], each with `order_id`, `order_date`, `total_amount`, `status`, `shipping_address`
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `orders-page`
  - Orders displayed in table with ID: `orders-table`
  - View order buttons: `view-order-button-{order_id}`
  - Dropdown filter for order status: `order-status-filter` (All, Shipped, Delivered)
  - Button to dashboard: `back-to-dashboard`

### Reviews
- Route: `/reviews` (GET)
- Template: `reviews.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `reviews`: List[Dict], each with book rating, review text
  - `books`: List[Dict] for filtering
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `reviews-page`
  - Div for all reviews with ID: `reviews-list`
  - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating: `filter-rating`
  - Button to write review: `write-review-button`

### Write Review
- Route: `/write_review` (GET, POST)
- Template: `write_review.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `books`: List[Dict]
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `write-review-page`
  - Dropdown select book: `select-book`
  - Rating select dropdown (1-5 stars): `rating-select`
  - Textarea for the review: `review-text`
  - Submit button: `submit-review-button`
- POST method to submit review

### Bestsellers
- Route: `/bestsellers` (GET)
- Template: `bestsellers.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `bestsellers`: List[Dict], each with `rank`, `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `sales_count`
  - `periods`: List[str]
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `bestsellers-page`
  - Div with ID: `bestsellers-list` containing ranked books
  - Dropdown to filter period: `period-filter`
  - View details buttons for books: `view-details-button-{book_id}`
  - Button to dashboard: `back-to-dashboard`


## 2. HTML Template Conventions (IDs and Elements)

- All pages include proper &lt;title&gt; tag as defined for that page.
- Main heading (h1) reflects the page title.
- Buttons and clickable elements have IDs as specified.
- Forms handling POST submissions have correct input controls and are clearly named according to variables.

## 3. Data Schemas

### books.txt
- Fields: `book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description`
- Example Data:
```
1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A novel about the American dream and social fiction.

```

- Example Data:

### orders.txt


### order_items.txt
- Fields: `order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price`

```
1|1|2|3|14.99
2|1|1|1|9.99
```

### reviews.txt

- Example Data:
```

3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and insightful.|2025-01-15
```

### bestsellers.txt

Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Bookstore Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured books, bestsellers, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-books** - Type: Div - Display of featured book recommendations.   - **ID: browse-catalog-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to book catalog page.   - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.   - **ID: bestsellers-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bestsellers page.  ### 2. Book Catalog Page - **Page Title**: Book Catalog - **Overview**: A page displaying all available books with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search books by title, author, or ISBN.   - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Fiction, Non-Fiction, Science, History, etc.).   - **ID: books-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying book cards with cover, title, author, and price.   - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each book card has this).  ### 3. Book Details Page - **Page Title**: Book Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific book. - **Elements**:   - **ID: book-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the book details page.   - **ID: book-title** - Type: H1 - Display book title.   - **ID: book-author** - Type: Div - Display book author.   - **ID: book-price** - Type: Div - Display book price.   - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add book to shopping cart.   - **ID: book-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.  ### 4. Shopping Cart Page - **Page Title**: Shopping Cart - **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option. - **Elements**:   - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.   - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with title, quantity, price, and subtotal.   - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).   - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).   - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.   - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.  ### 5. Checkout Page - **Page Title**: Checkout - **Overview**: A page for users to enter shipping information and complete purchase. - **Elements**:   - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.   - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.   - **ID: shipping-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input shipping address.   - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).   - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.  ### 6. Order History Page - **Page Title**: Order History - **Overview**: A page displaying all previous orders with tracking information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the orders page.   - **ID: orders-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.   - **ID: view-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view order details (each order has this).   - **ID: order-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Reviews Page - **Page Title**: Customer Reviews - **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews and allowing users to write new reviews. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.   - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with book title, rating, and review text.   - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.   - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Write Review Page - **Page Title**: Write a Review - **Overview**: A page for users to write reviews for purchased books. - **Elements**:   - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.   - **ID: select-book** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select book to review.   - **ID: rating-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).   - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.   - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.  ### 9. Bestsellers Page - **Page Title**: Bestsellers - **Overview**: A page displaying top-selling books ranked by sales. - **Elements**:   - **ID: bestsellers-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bestsellers page.   - **ID: bestsellers-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, and sales count.   - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (This Week, This Month, All Time).   - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each bestseller has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Books Data - **File Name**: `books.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel   2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind   3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction   ```  ### 2. Categories Data - **File Name**: `categories.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   category_id|category_name|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels   2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books   3|Science|Scientific topics and research   ```  ### 3. Cart Data - **File Name**: `cart.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2|2025-01-15   2|3|1|2025-01-16   ```  ### 4. Orders Data - **File Name**: `orders.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001   2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001   ```  ### 5. Order Items Data - **File Name**: `order_items.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2|12.99   2|1|3|1|14.99   3|2|2|1|16.99   ```  ### 6. Reviews Data - **File Name**: `reviews.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12   2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13   3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15   ```  ### 7. Bestsellers Data - **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   book_id|sales_count|period   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   2|150|This Month   1|120|This Month   3|95|This Month   ```
  [design_spec.md] # BookstoreOnline Flask Application Design Specification  ## 1. Flask Routes  ### Root Route - `/` (GET): redirects to `/dashboard`.  ### Dashboard - Route: `/dashboard` (GET) - Template: `dashboard.html` - Context Variables:   - `featured_books`: List[Dict], each dict contains `book_id` (int), `title` (str), `author` (str), `price` (float) - Purpose: Display featured recommendations with quick navigation. - Elements:   - Container with ID: `dashboard-page`   - Display container with ID: `featured-books`   - Button with ID: `browse-catalog-button` (Navigates to `/catalog`)  ### Catalog - Route: `/catalog` (GET) - Template: `catalog.html` - Context Variables:   - `books`: List[Dict], each with `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `category`, `price`   - `categories`: List[Dict], each with `category_id`, `category_name`, `description` - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `catalog-page`   - Search input text field: `search-input`   - Category filter dropdown: `category-filter`   - Book grid container: `book-grid`   - Each book card has an ID button: `view-details-button-{book_id}` - Features: Search by title or author; filter by category (e.g., Science)  ### Book Details - Route: `/book/<int:book_id>` (GET) - Template: `book_details.html` - Context Variables:   - `book`: Dict with detailed book information   - `reviews`: List[Dict] for the book - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `book-details-page`   - Book title display (H1 inside main heading)   - Div with ID: `book-price` to show price   - Button with ID: `add-to-cart-button` to add book to cart   - Div with ID: `book-reviews` to display customer reviews - Form for POST to add to cart  ### Shopping Cart - Route: `/cart` (GET, POST) - Template: `cart.html` - Context Variables:   - `cart_items`: List[Dict], each with `item_id`, `book`, `quantity`   - `total_amount`: Float - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `cart-page`   - Cart items displayed in table with ID: `cart-table`   - Quantity input fields: `update-quantity-{item_id}`   - Remove buttons: `remove-item-button-{item_id}`   - Div with ID: `total-amount` showing total cost   - Button to checkout: `checkout-button` - POST method handles quantity updates, removals  ### Checkout - Route: `/checkout` (GET, POST) - Template: `checkout.html` - Context Variables:   - `cart_items`, `total_amount` - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `checkout-page`   - Input field with ID: `shipping-address` for shipping info   - Payment method dropdown `payment-method` (e.g., Credit Card, PayPal)   - Button to place order: `place-order-button` - POST method processes order submission  ### Order History - Route: `/orders` (GET) - Template: `orders.html` - Context Variables:   - `orders`: List[Dict], each with `order_id`, `order_date`, `total_amount`, `status`, `shipping_address` - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `orders-page`   - Orders displayed in table with ID: `orders-table`   - View order buttons: `view-order-button-{order_id}`   - Dropdown filter for order status: `order-status-filter` (All, Shipped, Delivered)   - Button to dashboard: `back-to-dashboard`  ### Reviews - Route: `/reviews` (GET) - Template: `reviews.html` - Context Variables:   - `reviews`: List[Dict], each with book rating, review text   - `books`: List[Dict] for filtering - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `reviews-page`   - Div for all reviews with ID: `reviews-list`   - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating: `filter-rating`   - Button to write review: `write-review-button`  ### Write Review - Route: `/write_review` (GET, POST) - Template: `write_review.html` - Context Variables:   - `books`: List[Dict] - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `write-review-page`   - Dropdown select book: `select-book`   - Rating select dropdown (1-5 stars): `rating-select`   - Textarea for the review: `review-text`   - Submit button: `submit-review-button` - POST method to submit review  ### Bestsellers - Route: `/bestsellers` (GET) - Template: `bestsellers.html` - Context Variables:   - `bestsellers`: List[Dict], each with `rank`, `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `sales_count`   - `periods`: List[str] - Elements:   - Container div with ID: `bestsellers-page`   - Div with ID: `bestsellers-list` containing ranked books   - Dropdown to filter period: `period-filter`   - View details buttons for books: `view-details-button-{book_id}`   - Button to dashboard: `back-to-dashboard`   ## 2. HTML Template Conventions (IDs and Elements)  - All pages include proper &lt;title&gt; tag as defined for that page. - Main heading (h1) reflects the page title. - Buttons and clickable elements have IDs as specified. - Forms handling POST submissions have correct input controls and are clearly named according to variables.  ## 3. Data Schemas  ### books.txt - Fields: `book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description` - Example Data: ``` 1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A novel about the American dream and social fiction. 2|Brief History of Humankind|Yuval Noah Harari|9780143128540|Science|15.99|30|A brief history of humankind's evolution. 3|Astrophysics for People in a Hurry|Neil deGrasse Tyson|9780393609394|Science|14.99|40|A concise introduction to astrophysics. ```  ### categories.txt - Fields: `category_id|category_name|description` - Example Data: ``` 1|Fiction|Fiction books including classics and modern literature. 2|History|History and historical nonfiction. 3|Science|Scientific research and popular science books. ```  ### cart.txt - Fields: `cart_item_id|user_id|book_id|quantity|date_added` - Example Data: ``` 1|1|2|2|2025-01-15 2|1|3|1|2025-01-16 ```  ### orders.txt - Fields: `order_id|user_id|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address` - Example Data: ``` 1|1|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, York 2|2|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak St, Los Angeles, CA ```  ### order_items.txt - Fields: `order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price` - Example Data: ``` 1|1|2|3|14.99 2|1|1|1|9.99 ```  ### reviews.txt - Fields: `review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date` - Example Data: ``` 1|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13 3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and insightful.|2025-01-15 ```  ### bestsellers.txt - Fields: `book_id|sales_count|period` - Example Data: ``` 2|150|This Month 3|95|This Month ```   -- End of design_spec.md --

# Requirements Document for 'BookstoreOnline' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'BookstoreOnline' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse books, add items to cart, checkout, write reviews, and track order history. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'BookstoreOnline' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'BookstoreOnline' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Bookstore Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured books, bestsellers, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-books** - Type: Div - Display of featured book recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-catalog-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to book catalog page.
  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bestsellers page.

### 2. Book Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Book Catalog
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available books with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search books by title, author, or ISBN.
  - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Fiction, Non-Fiction, Science, History, etc.).
  - **ID: books-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying book cards with cover, title, author, and price.
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each book card has this).

### 3. Book Details Page
- **Page Title**: Book Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific book.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: book-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the book details page.
  - **ID: book-title** - Type: H1 - Display book title.
  - **ID: book-author** - Type: Div - Display book author.
  - **ID: book-price** - Type: Div - Display book price.
  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add book to shopping cart.
  - **ID: book-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Shopping Cart Page
- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart
- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.
  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with title, quantity, price, and subtotal.
  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.
  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.

### 5. Checkout Page
- **Page Title**: Checkout
- **Overview**: A page for users to enter shipping information and complete purchase.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.
  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: shipping-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input shipping address.
  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).
  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.

### 6. Order History Page
- **Page Title**: Order History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous orders with tracking information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the orders page.
  - **ID: orders-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.
  - **ID: view-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view order details (each order has this).
  - **ID: order-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reviews Page
- **Page Title**: Customer Reviews
- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews and allowing users to write new reviews.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.
  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with book title, rating, and review text.
  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.
  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Write Review Page
- **Page Title**: Write a Review
- **Overview**: A page for users to write reviews for purchased books.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.
  - **ID: select-book** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select book to review.
  - **ID: rating-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).
  - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.
  - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.

### 9. Bestsellers Page
- **Page Title**: Bestsellers
- **Overview**: A page displaying top-selling books ranked by sales.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: bestsellers-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bestsellers page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, and sales count.
  - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (This Week, This Month, All Time).
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each bestseller has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Books Data
- **File Name**: `books.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- **File Name**: `categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
  3|Science|Scientific topics and research
  ```

### 3. Cart Data
- **File Name**: `cart.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2|2025-01-15
  2|3|1|2025-01-16
  ```

### 4. Orders Data
- **File Name**: `orders.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
  ```

### 5. Order Items Data
- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2|12.99
  2|1|3|1|14.99
  3|2|2|1|16.99
  ```

### 6. Reviews Data
- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
  ```

### 7. Bestsellers Data
- **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|sales_count|period
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  2|150|This Month
  1|120|This Month
  3|95|This Month
  ```


=== design_spec.md ===
# BookstoreOnline Flask Application Design Specification

## 1. Flask Routes

### Root Route
- `/` (GET): redirects to `/dashboard`.

### Dashboard
- Route: `/dashboard` (GET)
- Template: `dashboard.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `featured_books`: List[Dict], each dict contains `book_id` (int), `title` (str), `author` (str), `price` (float)
- Purpose: Display featured recommendations with quick navigation.
- Elements:
  - Container with ID: `dashboard-page`
  - Display container with ID: `featured-books`
  - Button with ID: `browse-catalog-button` (Navigates to `/catalog`)

### Catalog
- Route: `/catalog` (GET)
- Template: `catalog.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `books`: List[Dict], each with `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `category`, `price`
  - `categories`: List[Dict], each with `category_id`, `category_name`, `description`
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `catalog-page`
  - Search input text field: `search-input`
  - Category filter dropdown: `category-filter`
  - Book grid container: `book-grid`
  - Each book card has an ID button: `view-details-button-{book_id}`
- Features: Search by title or author; filter by category (e.g., Science)

### Book Details
- Route: `/book/<int:book_id>` (GET)
- Template: `book_details.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `book`: Dict with detailed book information
  - `reviews`: List[Dict] for the book
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `book-details-page`
  - Book title display (H1 inside main heading)
  - Div with ID: `book-price` to show price
  - Button with ID: `add-to-cart-button` to add book to cart
  - Div with ID: `book-reviews` to display customer reviews
- Form for POST to add to cart

### Shopping Cart
- Route: `/cart` (GET, POST)
- Template: `cart.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `cart_items`: List[Dict], each with `item_id`, `book`, `quantity`
  - `total_amount`: Float
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `cart-page`
  - Cart items displayed in table with ID: `cart-table`
  - Quantity input fields: `update-quantity-{item_id}`
  - Remove buttons: `remove-item-button-{item_id}`
  - Div with ID: `total-amount` showing total cost
  - Button to checkout: `checkout-button`
- POST method handles quantity updates, removals

### Checkout
- Route: `/checkout` (GET, POST)
- Template: `checkout.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `cart_items`, `total_amount`
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `checkout-page`
  - Input field with ID: `shipping-address` for shipping info
  - Payment method dropdown `payment-method` (e.g., Credit Card, PayPal)
  - Button to place order: `place-order-button`
- POST method processes order submission

### Order History
- Route: `/orders` (GET)
- Template: `orders.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `orders`: List[Dict], each with `order_id`, `order_date`, `total_amount`, `status`, `shipping_address`
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `orders-page`
  - Orders displayed in table with ID: `orders-table`
  - View order buttons: `view-order-button-{order_id}`
  - Dropdown filter for order status: `order-status-filter` (All, Shipped, Delivered)
  - Button to dashboard: `back-to-dashboard`

### Reviews
- Route: `/reviews` (GET)
- Template: `reviews.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `reviews`: List[Dict], each with book rating, review text
  - `books`: List[Dict] for filtering
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `reviews-page`
  - Div for all reviews with ID: `reviews-list`
  - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating: `filter-rating`
  - Button to write review: `write-review-button`

### Write Review
- Route: `/write_review` (GET, POST)
- Template: `write_review.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `books`: List[Dict]
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `write-review-page`
  - Dropdown select book: `select-book`
  - Rating select dropdown (1-5 stars): `rating-select`
  - Textarea for the review: `review-text`
  - Submit button: `submit-review-button`
- POST method to submit review

### Bestsellers
- Route: `/bestsellers` (GET)
- Template: `bestsellers.html`
- Context Variables:
  - `bestsellers`: List[Dict], each with `rank`, `book_id`, `title`, `author`, `sales_count`
  - `periods`: List[str]
- Elements:
  - Container div with ID: `bestsellers-page`
  - Div with ID: `bestsellers-list` containing ranked books
  - Dropdown to filter period: `period-filter`
  - View details buttons for books: `view-details-button-{book_id}`
  - Button to dashboard: `back-to-dashboard`


## 2. HTML Template Conventions (IDs and Elements)

- All pages include proper &lt;title&gt; tag as defined for that page.
- Main heading (h1) reflects the page title.
- Buttons and clickable elements have IDs as specified.
- Forms handling POST submissions have correct input controls and are clearly named according to variables.

## 3. Data Schemas

### books.txt
- Fields: `book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description`
- Example Data:
```
1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A novel about the American dream and social fiction.
2|Brief History of Humankind|Yuval Noah Harari|9780143128540|Science|15.99|30|A brief history of humankind's evolution.
3|Astrophysics for People in a Hurry|Neil deGrasse Tyson|9780393609394|Science|14.99|40|A concise introduction to astrophysics.
```

### categories.txt
- Fields: `category_id|category_name|description`
- Example Data:
```
1|Fiction|Fiction books including classics and modern literature.
2|History|History and historical nonfiction.
3|Science|Scientific research and popular science books.
```

### cart.txt
- Fields: `cart_item_id|user_id|book_id|quantity|date_added`
- Example Data:
```
1|1|2|2|2025-01-15
2|1|3|1|2025-01-16
```

### orders.txt
- Fields: `order_id|user_id|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address`
- Example Data:
```
1|1|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, York
2|2|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak St, Los Angeles, CA
```

### order_items.txt
- Fields: `order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price`
- Example Data:
```
1|1|2|3|14.99
2|1|1|1|9.99
```

### reviews.txt
- Fields: `review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date`
- Example Data:
```
1|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and insightful.|2025-01-15
```

### bestsellers.txt
- Fields: `book_id|sales_count|period`
- Example Data:
```
2|150|This Month
3|95|This Month
```

# Requirements Document for 'BookstoreOnline' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'BookstoreOnline' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse books, add items to cart, checkout, write reviews, and track order history. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'BookstoreOnline' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'BookstoreOnline' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Bookstore Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured books, bestsellers, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-books** - Type: Div - Display of featured book recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-catalog-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to book catalog page.
  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bestsellers page.

### 2. Book Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Book Catalog
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available books with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search books by title, author, or ISBN.
  - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Fiction, Non-Fiction, Science, History, etc.).
  - **ID: books-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying book cards with cover, title, author, and price.
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each book card has this).

### 3. Book Details Page
- **Page Title**: Book Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific book.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: book-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the book details page.
  - **ID: book-title** - Type: H1 - Display book title.
  - **ID: book-author** - Type: Div - Display book author.
  - **ID: book-price** - Type: Div - Display book price.
  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add book to shopping cart.
  - **ID: book-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Shopping Cart Page
- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart
- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.
  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with title, quantity, price, and subtotal.
  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.
  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.

### 5. Checkout Page
- **Page Title**: Checkout
- **Overview**: A page for users to enter shipping information and complete purchase.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.
  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: shipping-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input shipping address.
  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).
  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.

### 6. Order History Page
- **Page Title**: Order History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous orders with tracking information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the orders page.
  - **ID: orders-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.
  - **ID: view-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view order details (each order has this).
  - **ID: order-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reviews Page
- **Page Title**: Customer Reviews
- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews and allowing users to write new reviews.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.
  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with book title, rating, and review text.
  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.
  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Write Review Page
- **Page Title**: Write a Review
- **Overview**: A page for users to write reviews for purchased books.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.
  - **ID: select-book** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select book to review.
  - **ID: rating-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).
  - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.
  - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.

### 9. Bestsellers Page
- **Page Title**: Bestsellers
- **Overview**: A page displaying top-selling books ranked by sales.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: bestsellers-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bestsellers page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, and sales count.
  - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (This Week, This Month, All Time).
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each bestseller has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Books Data
- **File Name**: `books.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- **File Name**: `categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
  3|Science|Scientific topics and research
  ```

### 3. Cart Data
- **File Name**: `cart.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2|2025-01-15
  2|3|1|2025-01-16
  ```

### 4. Orders Data
- **File Name**: `orders.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
  ```

### 5. Order Items Data
- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2|12.99
  2|1|3|1|14.99
  3|2|2|1|16.99
  ```

### 6. Reviews Data
- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
  ```

### 7. Bestsellers Data
- **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|sales_count|period
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  2|150|This Month
  1|120|This Month
  3|95|This Month
  ```

`cart-page` (main container div)\n  - For each item:\n    - `update-quantity-{item_id}` (input field for qty)\n    - `remove-item-button-{item_id}` (button)\n  - `total-amount` (span showing total)\n  - `checkout-page` (container div)\n  - `shipping-address` (textarea for shipping info)\n  - `payment-method` (dropdown: Credit Card, PayPal,...)\n  - `place-order-button` (button to submit order)\n- Form method POST\n\n### orders.html\n- Title: `<title>Order History</title>`\n- Heading: `<h1>Order History</h1>`\n- IDs:\n  - `orders-page` (container)\n  - `orders-table` (table listing orders)\n  - Each order row has `view-order-button-{order_id}` button\n  - `order-status-filter` (dropdown to filter by order status)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n\n### reviews.html\n- Title: `<title>Reviews</title>`\n- Heading: `<h1>Customer Reviews</h1>`\n- IDs:\n  - `reviews-page` (main div)\n  - `reviews-list` (div, reviews displayed)\n  - `write-review-button` (button to `/write_review`)\n  - Filter options by rating, book, etc.\n\n### write_review.html\n- Title: `<title>Write Review</title>`\n- Heading: `<h1>Write a Review</h1>`\n- IDs:\n  - `bestsellers-page` (container)\n  - `bestsellers-list` (div of ranked books)\n  - `period-filter` (dropdown for period selection)\n  - Each book has `view-details-button-{book_id}`\n  - `back-to-dashboard` button\n\n\n## 3. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A novel about the American dream and social fiction.\n  2|Brief History of Humankind|Yuval Noah Harari|9780143128540|Science|15.99|30|A brief history of humankind's evolution.\n  3|Astrophysics for People in a Hurry|Neil deGrasse Tyson|9780393609394|Science|14.99|40|A concise introduction to astrophysics.\n  ```\n\n### categories.txt\n- File name: `categories.txt`\n- Format:\n  ```\n  category_id|category_name|description\n  ```\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|Fiction|Fiction books including classics and modern literature.\n  2|History|History and historical nonfiction.\n  3|Science|Scientific research and popular science books.\n  ```\n\n### cart.txt\n- File name: `cart.txt`\n- Format:\n  ```\n  cart_item_id|user_id|book_id|quantity|date_added\n  ```\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|1|2|2|2025-01-15\n  2|1|3|1|2025-01-16\n  ```\n\n### orders.txt\n- File name: `orders.txt`\n- Format:\n  ```\n  order_id|user_id|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address\n  ```\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|1|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, York\n  2|2|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Los Angeles, CA\n  ```\n\n### order_items.txt\n- File name: `order_items.txt`\n- Format:\n  ```\n  order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price\n  ```\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|1|2|3|14.99\n  2|1|1|1|9.99\n  ```\n\n### reviews.txt\n- File name: `reviews.txt`\n- Format:\n  ```\n  review_id|book_id|reviewer_name|rating|review_text|review_date\n  ```\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13\n  2|3|Charlie Brown|5|A true classic and very insightful.|2025-01-15\n  ```\n\n### bestsellers.txt\n- File name: `bestsellers.txt`\n- Format:\n  ```\n  book_id|sales_count|period\n  ```\n- Description:\n  - `period` e.g. 'Month', 'Year'\n- Examples:\n  ```\n  1|150|Month\n  2|200|Month\n  ```\n\n\n---\nThis completes the detailed design specification for the BookstoreOnline Flask application.\n"})

=== user_task_description ===

# Requirements Document for 'BookstoreOnline' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'BookstoreOnline' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse books, add items to cart, checkout, write reviews, and track order history. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'BookstoreOnline' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'BookstoreOnline' web application will consist of the following nine pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Bookstore Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured books, bestsellers, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-books** - Type: Div - Display of featured book recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-catalog-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to book catalog page.
  - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bestsellers page.

### 2. Book Catalog Page
- **Page Title**: Book Catalog
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available books with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search books by title, author, or ISBN.
  - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Fiction, Non-Fiction, Science, History, etc.).
  - **ID: books-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying book cards with cover, title, author, and price.
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each book card has this).

### 3. Book Details Page
- **Page Title**: Book Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific book.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: book-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the book details page.
  - **ID: book-title** - Type: H1 - Display book title.
  - **ID: book-author** - Type: Div - Display book author.
  - **ID: book-price** - Type: Div - Display book price.
  - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add book to shopping cart.
  - **ID: book-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.

### 4. Shopping Cart Page
- **Page Title**: Shopping Cart
- **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.
  - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with title, quantity, price, and subtotal.
  - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).
  - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.
  - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.

### 5. Checkout Page
- **Page Title**: Checkout
- **Overview**: A page for users to enter shipping information and complete purchase.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.
  - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: shipping-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input shipping address.
  - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).
  - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.

### 6. Order History Page
- **Page Title**: Order History
- **Overview**: A page displaying all previous orders with tracking information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the orders page.
  - **ID: orders-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.
  - **ID: view-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view order details (each order has this).
  - **ID: order-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Reviews Page
- **Page Title**: Customer Reviews
- **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews and allowing users to write new reviews.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.
  - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with book title, rating, and review text.
  - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.
  - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Write Review Page
- **Page Title**: Write a Review
- **Overview**: A page for users to write reviews for purchased books.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.
  - **ID: select-book** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select book to review.
  - **ID: rating-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).
  - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.
  - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.

### 9. Bestsellers Page
- **Page Title**: Bestsellers
- **Overview**: A page displaying top-selling books ranked by sales.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: bestsellers-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bestsellers page.
  - **ID: bestsellers-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, and sales count.
  - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (This Week, This Month, All Time).
  - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each bestseller has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Books Data
- **File Name**: `books.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel
  2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind
  3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction
  ```

### 2. Categories Data
- **File Name**: `categories.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  category_id|category_name|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels
  2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books
  3|Science|Scientific topics and research
  ```

### 3. Cart Data
- **File Name**: `cart.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2|2025-01-15
  2|3|1|2025-01-16
  ```

### 4. Orders Data
- **File Name**: `orders.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001
  2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001
  ```

### 5. Order Items Data
- **File Name**: `order_items.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|1|2|12.99
  2|1|3|1|14.99
  3|2|2|1|16.99
  ```

### 6. Reviews Data
- **File Name**: `reviews.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12
  2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13
  3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15
  ```

### 7. Bestsellers Data
- **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  book_id|sales_count|period
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  2|150|This Month
  1|120|This Month
  3|95|This Month
  ```

  - Route path (including parameter syntax, e.g., /book/<int:book_id>)

2. **HTML Templates Specification**

Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'BookstoreOnline' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse books, add items to cart, checkout, write reviews, and track order history. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'BookstoreOnline' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'BookstoreOnline' web application will consist of the following nine pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Bookstore Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured books, bestsellers, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-books** - Type: Div - Display of featured book recommendations.   - **ID: browse-catalog-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to book catalog page.   - **ID: view-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to shopping cart page.   - **ID: bestsellers-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to bestsellers page.  ### 2. Book Catalog Page - **Page Title**: Book Catalog - **Overview**: A page displaying all available books with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: catalog-page** - Type: Div - Container for the catalog page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search books by title, author, or ISBN.   - **ID: category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Fiction, Non-Fiction, Science, History, etc.).   - **ID: books-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying book cards with cover, title, author, and price.   - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each book card has this).  ### 3. Book Details Page - **Page Title**: Book Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific book. - **Elements**:   - **ID: book-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the book details page.   - **ID: book-title** - Type: H1 - Display book title.   - **ID: book-author** - Type: Div - Display book author.   - **ID: book-price** - Type: Div - Display book price.   - **ID: add-to-cart-button** - Type: Button - Button to add book to shopping cart.   - **ID: book-reviews** - Type: Div - Section displaying customer reviews.  ### 4. Shopping Cart Page - **Page Title**: Shopping Cart - **Overview**: A page displaying items in the cart with quantity management and checkout option. - **Elements**:   - **ID: cart-page** - Type: Div - Container for the cart page.   - **ID: cart-items-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying cart items with title, quantity, price, and subtotal.   - **ID: update-quantity-{item_id}** - Type: Input (number) - Field to update item quantity (each cart item has this).   - **ID: remove-item-button-{item_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove item from cart (each cart item has this).   - **ID: proceed-checkout-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed to checkout.   - **ID: total-amount** - Type: Div - Display total cart amount.  ### 5. Checkout Page - **Page Title**: Checkout - **Overview**: A page for users to enter shipping information and complete purchase. - **Elements**:   - **ID: checkout-page** - Type: Div - Container for the checkout page.   - **ID: customer-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.   - **ID: shipping-address** - Type: Textarea - Field to input shipping address.   - **ID: payment-method** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select payment method (Credit Card, PayPal, Bank Transfer).   - **ID: place-order-button** - Type: Button - Button to confirm and place order.  ### 6. Order History Page - **Page Title**: Order History - **Overview**: A page displaying all previous orders with tracking information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: orders-page** - Type: Div - Container for the orders page.   - **ID: orders-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying orders with order ID, date, total amount, and status.   - **ID: view-order-button-{order_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view order details (each order has this).   - **ID: order-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Shipped, Delivered).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Reviews Page - **Page Title**: Customer Reviews - **Overview**: A page displaying all customer reviews and allowing users to write new reviews. - **Elements**:   - **ID: reviews-page** - Type: Div - Container for the reviews page.   - **ID: reviews-list** - Type: Div - List of all reviews with book title, rating, and review text.   - **ID: write-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to write review page.   - **ID: filter-by-rating** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter reviews by rating (All, 5 stars, 4 stars, etc.).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Write Review Page - **Page Title**: Write a Review - **Overview**: A page for users to write reviews for purchased books. - **Elements**:   - **ID: write-review-page** - Type: Div - Container for the write review page.   - **ID: select-book** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select book to review.   - **ID: rating-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select rating (1-5 stars).   - **ID: review-text** - Type: Textarea - Field to write review text.   - **ID: submit-review-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit review.  ### 9. Bestsellers Page - **Page Title**: Bestsellers - **Overview**: A page displaying top-selling books ranked by sales. - **Elements**:   - **ID: bestsellers-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bestsellers page.   - **ID: bestsellers-list** - Type: Div - Ranked list of bestselling books with rank, title, author, and sales count.   - **ID: time-period-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by time period (This Week, This Month, All Time).   - **ID: view-book-button-{book_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view book details (each bestseller has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'BookstoreOnline' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Books Data - **File Name**: `books.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   book_id|title|author|isbn|category|price|stock|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|The Great Gatsby|F. Scott Fitzgerald|9780743273565|Fiction|12.99|50|A classic American novel   2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|9780062316097|Non-Fiction|16.99|30|A brief history of humankind   3|1984|George Orwell|9780451524935|Fiction|14.99|45|Dystopian social science fiction   ```  ### 2. Categories Data - **File Name**: `categories.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   category_id|category_name|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Fiction|Fictional narratives and novels   2|Non-Fiction|Factual and educational books   3|Science|Scientific topics and research   ```  ### 3. Cart Data - **File Name**: `cart.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   cart_id|book_id|quantity|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2|2025-01-15   2|3|1|2025-01-16   ```  ### 4. Orders Data - **File Name**: `orders.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_id|customer_name|order_date|total_amount|status|shipping_address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|John Doe|2025-01-10|38.97|Delivered|123 Main St, New York, NY 10001   2|Jane Smith|2025-01-14|16.99|Shipped|456 Oak Ave, Los Angeles, CA 90001   ```  ### 5. Order Items Data - **File Name**: `order_items.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   order_item_id|order_id|book_id|quantity|price   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|1|2|12.99   2|1|3|1|14.99   3|2|2|1|16.99   ```  ### 6. Reviews Data - **File Name**: `reviews.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   review_id|book_id|customer_name|rating|review_text|review_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|5|Amazing book! A true classic.|2025-01-12   2|2|Bob Williams|4|Very informative and well-written.|2025-01-13   3|3|Charlie Brown|5|Thought-provoking and relevant today.|2025-01-15   ```  ### 7. Bestsellers Data - **File Name**: `bestsellers.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   book_id|sales_count|period   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   2|150|This Month   1|120|This Month   3|95|This Month   ```
